< review>
One star is too generous for this "facility."  I recently needed to utilize local agencies to ensure the safety of a loved one and based on the persistent suicidal ideation that was being expressed, the decision was made to send them to ETS for psychiatric "care."  Care is the absolute last thing on their mind.   Before my relative was admitted I inquired about the necessity of a consent form being signed and I was told twice that it wasn't necessary.  However, once I attempted to get in touch with my relative, I was told that I couldn't get any information at all because a consent form wasn't signed.  Despite that, when I called around to the different departments/buildings, I was told that my relative was in the general holding area and that if I wanted to talk with my relative I "may or may not" be able to talk with them because the patients are the ones who answer the phone in the holding area and its up to the patients to get the phone to the person being contacted.  After no success during that first attempt I called back only to be shuffled around to all of the different departments again and even after initially being told that my relative was in the holding area, this time I was told in each department that my relative could not be located. The last employee that I spoke with literally said "yeah, I don't know what to tell you" when I asked about some type of solution.  I had to contact my insurance to get my relative moved to a different facility just for peace of mind.  Never again in my life will I allow any person that I care about to go to that facility, EVER!  I would rather drive to San Diego County in order to get them treated at another facility despite the problem than to subject anyone to this place!< /review>

< Review>
NO STARS would be more accurate. I have to say this is a hell hole, a traumatizing horrific place. It is overcrowded ( mostly by homeless drug addicts, and alcoholics )  staffed by people who speak with thick, heavy, hard to understand accents. Most of the staff is uncaring, detached, unresponsive and neglectful, with some exceptions. There was only one psychiatrist for over 40 patients. I was wrongfully sent there ( from a phone conversation with a spiteful landlord who gave a false report to the police) and I was held illegally for 25 hours. The only reason I was discharged is that after 16 hours one nurse actually listened to me, verified my explanation, and urged the second doctor ( I had to wait 25 hours to see him) to discharge me, who after listening to me for 4 minutes did release me immediately. Conditions are horrible, no real beds except in 2 isolation rooms, no privacy, no one tells you what the rules are, but the first "doctor" I spoke to, after 4 hours of waiting for an evaluation, informed me that I would remain in lock up for a mandatory 72 hours and there is a possibility  of an additional 14 DAYS if I do not obey the rules. I asked her what these rules are, as no one had explained any to me. She ignored the question and told me there were 6 pages she had to fill in. Upon entry it was clear that we were in for something special. The bar served top shelf beverages and featured drinks. The live entertainment blended perfectly in the background.  We were lucky enough to be invited guests of a 24 Carrots hosted event.  We have been to many events where 24 Carrots catered and been incredibly impressed every time.  Last night was no different. The tables were beautifully set very formally. It was a five course dinner with countless servers tending to every detail. If you are looking for a venue for a special event, or to have your event catered in a way that's sure to impress,  you have to check out Franciscan Gardens and 24 Carrots!</Review>

<review>This is such a beautiful venue for a wedding! There is an indoor and outdoor area but the outdoor part is definitely my favorite. It can be used for both the ceremony and reception, but it's nice to have an indoor option in case of rain. My one complaint about this venue is the lack of natural light in the getting ready rooms (there's no windows) but that's a small detail and it wasn't too dark for pictures or anything. The San Juan Mission is located just down the street and is a great place to go for couples portraits on the wedding day. Overall my experience here as a wedding photographer was a good one! One other thing for anyone planning to come here - the venue can be easy to miss on your first visit as it is along a busy-ish street and to get to the parking area you pull into what seems like an alley but if you look for a sign, there is one that says "Franciscan Gardens" hanging on the front of the building. Photos below by Carrie Rogers Photography</review>< user>

< review>
4.5 stars. Hmm where do I begin? Anyways, was down here for some stuff and a lot of people told me that this place was amazing, so I was like "I'll try it,". It was about 7 when I got there and there was a line outside the store. I was like," How long would this take,", but the line moved quickly( I would say there were about 10 people outside including me). It took about 10 minutes to get in. The inside is small, clean, and quite warm. Not many seats, but I guess most people just get out once they buy stuff. I was recommended by my friends to try the Macaron ice cream sandwiches that they had to offer( and yes I do like macarons). So I got the Red Velvet macaron sandwich. It was $6, and the size of your hand. Anyways, I took a bite and I was in love. The macaron shell was nice. It had the feet, was soft, but chewy, and delicious, though it didn't really taste like red velvet( it was still good though). The ice cream was delicious. Cold, sweet, creamy, perfectly molded, and had pieces of red velvet( I think). Half of it was dipped in white chocolate which made it more amazing. Presentation was also awesome! I would definitely come back when I am in the area. :) See ya soon!<//review>

<review>Can't say more positive things about this place. Tina was incredibly knowledgeable, friendly, and proficient.

This place is a little hard to find, as it's inside a plaza within a shopping center. You can't see the store from the parking lot -- you have to walk past the Stone Creek Plaza sign and look to your right on the first floor.

Tina explained to me all the mistakes my last barber made -- spoiler alert: there was a lot. That's what I get for going to a really cheap, $8 place.

She corrected it the best she could and explained to me the best way to cut my thick, coarse, Asian hair. She was disappointed in my prior cut, which just shows how much she cares about her craft. Really cool to see. She said that they would love to have me back in the future, which was also very nice.

She even recommended a nearby Tiawanese place I'm going to try. And then to top it off, she gave me a tub of gel to aid my reeling, recovering hair.

Best barber I've ever had, by far. I know you read that in pretty much 40% of barber reviews -- seriously, do the math -- but this place it's actually true. I'll be back again!< /review>< rate>

<text>This place has a really cool vibe. I have been here twice. Both times I ordered their big Crispy Chicken Sandwich it tastes hand breaded and was consistently delicious. The bbq sauce is spot on amazing. The fries are always hot and seasoned perfectly. Their crispy chicken sandwich alone will have me coming back for more.
At first it is a bit awkward having to give the cashier your phone number to be sent a text when your order is ready. (Had to do this both times) There are tablets to the right of the entrance for quick ordering. It was on the pricey side as the burgers and sandwiches do not come with fries and a drink. It would be helpful if there was a combo option without having to pay the separate charge for adding both. There are a few vegetarian options on the menu such as a black bean burger, salads, onion rings and fries. There is a dessert menu with milk shakes and soft serve. The kids menu has a variety of entrees to match with fries or fruit. There is beer on tap with a rotating seasonal selection. The wait for the food was no more than 15-20 minutes. There is a small section for patio seating outside. Seating inside could be greatly improved there are some booths along the back wall, but most of the main seating feels crowded. <user>100669041324793972979</user>< Name>
Jordan Bradley< /Name>
<Date>1571612112868< /Date><Rate>4<//Rate><Review>The Hangar is a great place to grab drinks and watch the game or grab a quick bite before the movies.

Upon first glance, I initially thought The Hangar was your run-of-the-mill chain restaurant that just ended up in Fresno. By the end of my meal, I realized how wrong I was.

The Hanger is exclusive to Fresno and owned by a small business owner. It specializes in carnival-type food and was inspired by Disneyland's soaring over CA ride. On the menu you'll find American comforts ranging from Bacon Cheeseburgers to Chili Dogs to Banana Split Sundays. Around the restaurant, you'll notice plane themed bars, fans, and decor. Theres even a huge mural, done by a local artist, that you can take a pic in front of that makes it look as if you've just parachuted into town!

All in all it was a really good a experience and the food was just as I expected. Nothing more, nothing less. The Tri-tip sandwich is a must-have. They make their own bbq in-house and it reminds me of a tangy sweet sauce similar to the BBQ sauce found in Lucille's BBQ chain. I also ordered a chili dog since I'm a fan of all things hotdog. The chili was a savory meat based chili and it sat over an Angus dog on a bulky bun. I ended up having to eat it with a fork and knife, but I finished every last bite. I also saw many people ordering milkshakes and sundaes. Those people told me that next time I'd HAVE to grab one as they were also delicous.

The service was also very smooth. They use a smart system that will text you when your order is ready. I found it to be very useful as I could shop around and didnt have to hover around the food counter. The staff, called flight attendants, were also very very kind and helpful. They routinely came around to the table asking if anyone needed anything and cleaning up small spills.

In conclusion, I'm glad Frenso finally got something fresh and orginal in the from of The Hangar. I would definitely recommend this place to anyone traveling from out of town or any local looking for something tasty and unique.<//Review>< pics>

<time>1467742232921< /time><rating>4<//rating><Text>An interestingly shaped park. It doesn't have much in the way of "grass" but does have a fairly quiet play area. The play area for the kids is small so two families would make it feel packed, but it feels sort of secluded hidden up the hill and in the trees. It is a bit of a walk to get to the play area, but it isn't bad. It's actually quite peaceful and due to it being at the top of a hill, you can get a really nice breeze. There is a bike path that runs through the park which goes quite a distance. I have never walked it to see how far it goes, but I suspect it is connected to most of Folsom via other bike paths.< /Text>< Pics>

< Review>
Nice park nestled in the Briggs Ranch development. There's street parking. You climb a little up a small hill to the two playground areas. The park also has two volleyball courts, barbecue grills, horseshoe toss set up, and a port-o-potty. Nice view of the surrounding hills. There are bike paths/walkways that connect to other parts of the neighborhood and the other city bike paths. It hasn't been too crowded the handful of times we've been there. Great place for the kids.<//Review>

<Text>Went to the Vestry for the first time this weekend and had a really great experience! It will def become one of my regular brunch spots in the mission. They have a lovely outdoor area as well as the indoor area. The bottomless mimosas are only $14 with food or $16 without food. The atmosphere is reach nice and the waitstaff were fairly attentive. The food was pretty good---didn't blow me away but def solid brunch food. I had the eggs benedict with avocado instead of ham and arugula instead of breakfast potatoes (I also appreciated that they were pretty accommodating with substitutes). But I would highly recommend the breakfast potatoes which were roasted in sea salt and rosemary and were oh so delicious! I also tried the flat bread---which I wasn't impressed with. The crust just didn't taste very good. All in all, I would def return--especially for a boozy brunch!<//Text>< Pics>

< review>
We stopped by for weekend brunch on the Vestry's outdoor patio. It's part of, and adjacent to, The Chapel, a sweet little music venue on Valencia between 18th & 19th. There is indoor seating as well, though it looked too dark and intimate for a sunny Sunday afternoon. We were seated in about 10 minutes; however service was unfortunately very slow - it took about 25 minutes from the time we were seated until someone took our orders. Luckily, the food came fairly quickly. The shrimp po-boy was tasty, if a bit bread-y. The accompanying slaw salad made up for the skimpiness of the shrimp. The homemade yogurt was a true standout, served in a mason jar, with granola, persimmons, and honey yogurt (which could be replaced by hemp seed or almond milk). The brunch prices are comparative to the area, at ~$8-$12 for most items. Tip: brunch selection is really more like lunch, meaning those who crave egg dishes and french toast may be disappointed.< /review>

< Review>
If you're planning to go to Antelope Valley Mall, the best spot to park at is by Macy's, either side. We also enjoy a brief walk on their halls to go through the other parts of the mall. They usually don't have the items that we're looking for, rarely they have it online too. But that does not mean they can't give 5 star service and quality products. They have a wide variety of branded goods so you can feel good of yourself. Avail of their cards to get discounts. We're not rich but we can afford their offerings via discounts and sales. As a matter of fact, if something is available on other shops in that same mall, Macy's gives them on discounted price. Who doesn't love that?< /Review>

< Text>
The store was clean and well-maintained.
Prices were higher than I expected after all this time. The sale prices on Levi's were good, though. I hadn't planned to go to the mall and wasn't really dressed for it (still had on pandemic-wear and was picking up food for some friends), and when I walked in the employee that greets you near the doors made me feel very uncomfortable. I won't be returning there for a good long time!
